                       <div data-reactid="2079">
                        <div data-reactid="2080">
                         30 acres of: great views, serenity, hiking/horse trails, and off the grid mountaintop living. Was a Civil War encampment with fortifications used in the "Battle of Resaca". Has PRIVACY with a MOUNTAIN TOP location. Stay in the coziness of a VINTAGE AIRSTREAM. Refurbished with wood floors, original wood cabinets, kitchen, all in perfect condition. On a gated private road with no other people but the owners down the hill who seldom travel on the road. HORSES CAN BE STABLED FOR RIDING TRAILS.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2081">
                         The Airstream, of course, has every amenity you need for "off grid" living. Cooking is on a propane stove. A full size refrigerator with ample freezer and cool storage for a family's groceries. Hot water is ample for a cleansing shower after a day of hiking or just relaxing outside in the shade. Peace and quiet is only limited to the noise you make. Outside is a firepit with ample firewood for your use. Sit at the picnic table or pull up one of the lawn chairs to add to your outdoor pleasure. We are proud of our rural setting and it's natural beauty. Enjoy it by relaxing in or out of the trailer, hiking, riding your horse, or going to one of the nearby towns. PLEASE NOTE: Water is limited to what is in your tank. "Electricity" is 12V and battery powered. Yes, you are "glamping". There is a generator to provide AC in the summer on a limited basis and to charge the batteries during the day. At other times, the batteries provide ample power; but as with everything, there are limits.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2082">
                         We are definitely rural. The closest grocery store is 18 or so miles away. Yes, there are a few convenience stores closer. Major hospitals are within 20 to 30 minutes. We are heavily forested and fires can be a major hazard. Bicycling is a major recreational pastime on our curvy roads. Be careful. Our neighbors are mainly agricultural. Their land is pretty much private; but there are miles and miles of national forest for your pleasure just to the west and north. Civil War reenactments are held in the spring and you need to look up "Battle of Resaca", Tunnel Hill, and Chickamagua to name just a few. Hiking is all around. Keown Falls, The Pocket, John's Mountain, Chestnut Mountain, Dry Creek, and many more trails. Check out: (URL HIDDEN)
                        </div>
